===================================================================================================================================
EFFECTS DATA FILE
===================================================================================================================================

Start X, Start Y: 
  Starting position on the texture as a percentage of the total texture size. 

End X, End Y: 
  Ending position on the texture as a percentage of the total texture size. 

Src Blend, Dest Blend:
  Blend_Zero, Blend_One, Blend_SrcColor, Blend_InvSrcColor, Blend_SrcAlpha, 
  Blend_InvSrcAlpha, Blend_DestAlpha, Blend_InvDestAlpha, Blend_DestColor, 
  Blend_InvDestColor, Blend_SrcAlphaSat, Blend_BothSrcAlpha, Blend_BothInvSrcAlpha


===================================================================================================================================
